If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.

That office now has jurisdiction over your case. We sent you a notice that explains why we moved your case. Please follow the instructions in the notice. If you do not receive your notice by February 18, 2023, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request a copy of the notice. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.

SRC2290143129
On January 19, 2023, we denied your request for expedited processing of your I-485, Application to Register Permanent Residence or Adjust Status, Receipt Number SRC2290143129. We do not believe, based on a review of your request, that your case meets one or more of the expedite criteria and otherwise merits expedited processing. We review all expedite requests on a case-by-case basis, and we grant them at the discretion of the director. Information regarding the USCIS expedite policy, including the expedite criteria, is available at www.uscis.gov/forms/expedite-criteria. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.
SRC2290073289
On January 19, 2023, we received your request for expedited processing on your Form I-485, Application to Register Permanent Residence or Adjust Status, Receipt Number SRC2290073289. We are reviewing your request and will notify you if we need additional information. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.
SRC2290047985
On January 19, 2023, we received your request to withdraw your Form I-485, Application to Register Permanent Residence or Adjust Status, Receipt Number SRC2290047985, and completed our review. We mailed you a Withdrawal Acknowledgment Notice. If you do not receive your Withdrawal Acknowledgment Notice by February 18, 2023, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request a copy of the notice. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.

If you do not receive your document by February 18, 2023, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request the document be sent to you. SRC2290010952
On January 19, 2023, we sent a request for additional evidence for your Form I-485, Application to Register Permanent Residence or Adjust Status, Receipt Number SRC2290010952. The request for evidence explains what we need from you. We will not take action on your case until we receive the evidence or the deadline to submit it expires. Please follow the instructions in the request for evidence. If you do not receive your request for additional evidence by February 3, 2023, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request a copy. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.
